if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') != 'ead295ad5182bd38c87eea295a951260447e2f88') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'ead295ad5182bd38c87eea295a951260447e2f88') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'fdde80d23182d02a0aa42bd7241eae487a6d9028') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'ead295ad5182bd38c87eea295a951260447e2f88') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != '481cea279402eb9c53394a5405583a3dce21ca68') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '481cea279402eb9c53394a5405583a3dce21ca68') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '2f4895d4001fd94d13cb7b427489dbbf5fc70d14') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '481cea279402eb9c53394a5405583a3dce21ca68') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') != '7e2c47b8972c29ba2975613beec3c65ac7ccabf8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '7e2c47b8972c29ba2975613beec3c65ac7ccabf8') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== 'bcdf17ac9001aac9a3d74d7404c0cd7fa2d88c6e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '7e2c47b8972c29ba2975613beec3c65ac7ccabf8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/licenses')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/licenses');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('vendor/licenses')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/licenses');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/licenses') != '64e746e8a9c26f9465a795308437b2dcc40cc36b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/licenses', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/licenses');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '64e746e8a9c26f9465a795308437b2dcc40cc36b') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '8b4a94726f505c332c3e755cf86ad60a88c09ca9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/licenses');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/licenses');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/licenses')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/licenses', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '64e746e8a9c26f9465a795308437b2dcc40cc36b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 721\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 721') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
